          <td>
           The former soldier gazes up at the endless sky, wondering where to travel next. He is content in following his heart and the intense righteousness inside, even if he must carve out paths no others have dared to tread. After all, his journey has only just begun.

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Gameplay_Notes">
        Gameplay Notes
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Improv_Duo">
        Improv Duo
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <span class="image_link">
         <span class="tooltip" style="border-bottom: 0;">
          <span typeof="mw:File">
           <a href="/Status_Effects" title="Status Effects">
            <img class="mw-file-element" data-file-height="64" data-file-width="64" decoding="async" height="25" loading="lazy" src="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/5/58/Status_7825.png/25px-Status_7825.png" srcset="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/5/58/Status_7825.png/38px-Status_7825.png 1.5x, https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/5/58/Status_7825.png/50px-Status_7825.png 2x" width="25"/>
           </a>
          </span>
          <a href="/Status_Effects" title="Status Effects">
           Improv Duo
          </a>
          <span class="tooltiptext">
           Can gain effects from Juri's charge attack, skills, and support skills / After three turns: Juri and the ally's ATK is sharply boosted against a foe with Mood Changer effect (1 hit) (Can't be removed / Can't be extended)
           <br/>
           <span class="hr">
           </span>
           <strong>
            Duration
           </strong>
           : 4 turns
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
        grants the following effects after 3 turns:
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GameWith_1-3">
         <a href="#cite_note-GameWith-1">
          [1]
         </a>
        </sup>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <span class="image_link">
           <span class="tooltip" style="border-bottom: 0;">
            <span typeof="mw:File">
             <a href="/Assassin_(Buff)" title="Assassin (Buff)">
              <img class="mw-file-element" data-file-height="64" data-file-width="64" decoding="async" height="25" loading="lazy" src="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/d/d0/Status_1457.png/25px-Status_1457.png" srcset="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/d/d0/Status_1457.png/38px-Status_1457.png 1.5x, https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/d/d0/Status_1457.png/50px-Status_1457.png 2x" width="25"/>
             </a>
            </span>
            <a href="/Assassin_(Buff)" title="Assassin (Buff)">
             230% Assassin's Aim (Mood Changer) (1 time)
            </a>
            <span class="tooltiptext">
             ATK is boosted against a foe with Mood Changer effect
             <br/>
             <span class="hr">
             </span>
             <strong>
              Strength
             </strong>
             : 230%
             <span class="hr">
             </span>
             <strong>
              Multiplier
             </strong>
             :
             <a href="/Damage_Formula/Detailed_Damage_Formula#Assassin_boost" title="Damage Formula/Detailed Damage Formula">
              Assassin
             </a>
             <span class="hr">
             </span>
             <strong>
              Duration
             </strong>
             : 1 turn
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          .
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Duo_for_the_Ages">
        Duo for the Ages
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <span class="image_link">
         <span class="tooltip" style="border-bottom: 0;">
          <span typeof="mw:File">
           <a href="/Status_Effects" title="Status Effects">
            <img class="mw-file-element" data-file-height="64" data-file-width="64" decoding="async" height="25" loading="lazy" src="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/1/16/Status_3256_2.png/25px-Status_3256_2.png" srcset="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/1/16/Status_3256_2.png/38px-Status_3256_2.png 1.5x, https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/1/16/Status_3256_2.png/50px-Status_3256_2.png 2x" width="25"/>
           </a>
          </span>
          <a href="/Status_Effects" title="Status Effects">
           Mood Changer
          </a>
          <span class="tooltiptext">
           ATK and multiattack rate are lowered (Can't be removed)
           <br/>
           <span class="hr">
           </span>
           <strong>
            Duration
           </strong>
           : 2 turns
           <span class="hr">
           </span>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/Local_status_effect" title="Local status effect">
            Local status effect
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
        has the following effects:
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GameWith_1-4">
         <a href="#cite_note-GameWith-1">
          [1]
         </a>
        </sup>
        <ul>
         <li>
          25% ATK Down
         </li>
         <li>
          DA Down
         </li>
         <li>
          TA Down
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bonus_DMG_Stacking_Information">
        Bonus DMG Stacking Information
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        The following is a curated list of how different Bonus DMG sources interact with Juri (SSR)'s skills. Check
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/Bonus_DMG" title="Bonus DMG">
         Bonus DMG
        </a>
        for further information and a comprehensive list.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <div class="character__details character--element-water">
       <table class="wikitable mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="text-align:left; max-width: 650px;width:100%;">
        <tbody>
         <tr>
          <th colspan="3">
           <span typeof="mw:File">
            <a href="/Juri_(SSR)" title="Juri (SSR)">
             <img class="mw-file-element" data-file-height="86" data-file-width="86" decoding="async" height="25" loading="lazy" src="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/c/c1/Skill_charge_attack.png/25px-Skill_charge_attack.png" srcset="https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/c/c1/Skill_charge_attack.png/38px-Skill_charge_attack.png 1.5x, https://gbf.wiki/images/thumb/c/c1/Skill_charge_attack.png/50px-Skill_charge_attack.png 2x" width="25"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="image_link">
            <span class="tooltip">
             <a class="mw-selflink selflink">
              Doombreaker
             </a>
             <span class="tooltiptext" style="">
              <span class="tooltip">
               450%
               <span class="tooltiptext" style="">
                Massive
               </span>

             <tr>
              <td class="image_assets-raid-normal">

                </a>
               </span>

       <table class="wikitable" style="text-align: center; text-size-adjust: none; width: 100%;">
        <tbody>
         <tr>
          <td>
           This stripped-down armor is popular with many a sojourner. Its design may be lacking a certain something, but it's that honest simplicity that leaves people with such a good impression.
          </td>
         </tr>
        </tbody>
       </table>
